## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes API Server Admission Controller Chain

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the API server admission controller pipeline: the admission.Interface registration, the generic admission chain execution, the mutating admission ordering, and the validating admission webhook call.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],

  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

## Kubernetes API Server Admission Controller Pipeline

The pipeline spans these key areas in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/`:

### 1. `admission.Interface` Registration
- **`interfaces.go`** — defines `Interface`, `MutationInterface`, `ValidationInterface`, `PluginInitializer`
- **`plugins.go`** — `Plugins` struct with `Register()` factory map and `NewFromPlugins()` that builds the chain
- **`pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go`** — `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` for kube-specific plugins
- **`staging/.../server/plugins.go`** — generic apiserver plugin registration

### 2. Generic Admission Chain Execution
- **`chain.go`** — `chainAdmissionHandler` iterates all handlers, calling `Admit()` then `Validate()`
- **`reinvocation.go`** — `newReinvocationHandler` wraps the chain with re-invocation logic
- **`audit.go`** — audit decoration wrapper
- **`metrics/metrics.go`** — per-plugin metrics instrumentation

### 3. Mutating Admission Ordering
- **`plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go`** + **`dispatcher.go`** + **`reinvocationcontext.go`** — MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin
- **`plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go`** + **`dispatcher.go`** + **`reinvocationcontext.go`** — CEL-based MutatingAdmissionPolicy
- **`plugin/policy/mutating/patch/`** — patch types (JSON patch, structured merge diff)

### 4. Validating Admission Webhook Call
- **`plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go`** + **`dispatcher.go`** — ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin
- **`plugin/policy/validating/plugin.go`** + **`dispatcher.go`** + **`validator.go`** — CEL-based ValidatingAdmissionPolicy
- **`configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`** + **`validating_webhook_manager.go`** — live webhook config management

is defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go, which declares Interface, MutationInterface, ValidationInterface, and PluginInitializer. Plugin registration is managed via the Plugins struct in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go, which provides Register() to add named factory functions and NewFromPlugins() to instantiate the ordered chain. The generic apiserver registers plugins via staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go (RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins), and the kube-apiserver adds all kube-specific plugins in pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go and configures options in pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go.\\n\\n## 2. Generic Admission Chain Execution\\n\\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go implements chainAdmissionHandler, which iterates over all registered handlers invoking Admit() (for MutationInterface) and then Validate() (for ValidationInterface) on each. staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go wraps the chain in a reinvoker that re-invokes when webhooks request it. Metrics instrumentation is in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go. Audit decoration is in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/audit.go. Plugin initializers are in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/initializer/ and pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/.\\n\\n## 3. Mutating Admission Ordering\\n\\nThe MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go) implements MutationInterface and uses dispatcher.go to call mutating webhooks in order, with re-invocation via reinvocationcontext.go. The CEL-based MutatingAdmissionPolicy plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go) works similarly via its dispatcher and reinvocation context. The patch sub-package handles ApplyConfiguration and JSON patch mutations. The shared generic policy infrastructure (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/generic/) is shared between mutating and validating policy plugins.\\n\\n## 4. Validating Admission Webhook Call\\n\\nThe ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go) implements ValidationInterface and calls webhooks via dispatcher.go. The CEL-based ValidatingAdmissionPolicy plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/plugin.go) evaluates CEL expressions. Webhook configuration is maintained live via staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/ (mutating_webhook_manager.go, validating_webhook_manager.go). Shared webhook infrastructure (request building, match conditions, accessors, etc.) lives under staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/.\"\n}\n",

is defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go, which declares Interface, MutationInterface, ValidationInterface, and PluginInitializer. Plugin registration is managed via the Plugins struct in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go, which provides Register() to add named factory functions and NewFromPlugins() to instantiate the ordered chain. The generic apiserver registers plugins via staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go (RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins), and the kube-apiserver adds all kube-specific plugins in pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go and configures options in pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go.\\n\\n## 2. Generic Admission Chain Execution\\n\\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go implements chainAdmissionHandler, which iterates over all registered handlers invoking Admit() (for MutationInterface) and then Validate() (for ValidationInterface) on each. staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go wraps the chain in a reinvoker that re-invokes when webhooks request it. Metrics instrumentation is in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go. Audit decoration is in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/audit.go. Plugin initializers are in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/initializer/ and pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/.\\n\\n## 3. Mutating Admission Ordering\\n\\nThe MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go) implements MutationInterface and uses dispatcher.go to call mutating webhooks in order, with re-invocation via reinvocationcontext.go. The CEL-based MutatingAdmissionPolicy plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go) works similarly via its dispatcher and reinvocation context. The patch sub-package handles ApplyConfiguration and JSON patch mutations. The shared generic policy infrastructure (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/generic/) is shared between mutating and validating policy plugins.\\n\\n## 4. Validating Admission Webhook Call\\n\\nThe ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go) implements ValidationInterface and calls webhooks via dispatcher.go. The CEL-based ValidatingAdmissionPolicy plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/plugin.go) evaluates CEL expressions. Webhook configuration is maintained live via staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/ (mutating_webhook_manager.go, validating_webhook_manager.go). Shared webhook infrastructure (request building, match conditions, accessors, etc.) lives under staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/.\"\n}\n",
